Subject: Unable to bind sub-directory unless parent directory has r+w for
 'other' users
MIME-Version: 1.0
Content-Type: multipart/mixed; 
	boundary="----=_Part_2932_1888787896.1515783945684"

------=_Part_2932_1888787896.1515783945684
Content-Type: multipart/alternative; 
	boundary="----=_Part_2933_1786939740.1515783945717"

------=_Part_2933_1786939740.1515783945717

Content-Transfer-Encoding: 7bit

I'm using 2.4-dist, and this works:

oni:~ $ singularity --version
2.4-dist
oni:~ $ singularity exec --bind /mnt/disk8/genetics/archival/:test_dir:ro /
mnt/disk2/com/container-images/python2.7.simg python --version
Python 2.7.14

But in 2.4-1 and 2.4.2, it does not:
unicorn:~ $ singularity --version
2.4.1-dist
unicorn:~ $ singularity exec --bind /mnt/disk8/genetics/archival/:test_dir:ro 
/mnt/disk2/com/container-images/python2.7.simg python --version
ERROR  : There was an error binding the path /mnt/disk8/genetics/archival/: 
Permission denied
ABORT  : Retval = 255

However, if I step up one directory, I can bind:
unicorn:~ $ singularity --version
2.4.1-dist
unicorn:~ $ singularity exec --bind /mnt/disk8/genetics/:test_dir:ro /mnt/
disk2/com/container-images/python2.7.simg python --version
Python 2.7.14

The breakdown of permissions:

dr-xr-xr-x  7 root        root         1.0K Jan 11 10:14 disk8
drwxrwx--- 18 share_owner NGS_USERS    2.0K Jan 11 10:12 genetics
drwxrwxr-x  6 sheenams    NGS_USERS    1.0K Jan  3  2017 archival

So, what changed in v2.4.1 that has changed the way binding works? These 
examples are showing 2.4.1, but the same behavior is in 2.4.2. Here's the 
debug log:
